(stream.type === 'pipe') {\n   414→        stream.handle.close();\n   415→      }\n   416→    }\n   417→\n   418→    this._handle.close();\n   419→    this._handle = null;\n   420→    throw new ErrnoException(err, 'spawn');\n   421→  } else {\n   422→    process.nextTick(onSpawnNT, this);\n   423→  }\n   424→\n   425→  this.pid = this._handle.pid;\n   426→\n   427→  for (i = 0; i < stdio.length; i++) {\n   428→    const stream = stdio[i];\n   429→    if (stream.type === 'ignore') continue;\n   430→\n   431→    if (stream.ipc) {\n   432→      this._closesNeeded++;\n   433→ time\n   438→    // the child process does.\n   439→    if (stream.type === 'wrap') {\n   440→      stream.handle.reading = false;\n   441→      stream.handle.readStop();\n   442→ (i > 0 && this.pid !== 0) {\n   454→        this._closesNeeded++;\n   455→        stream.socket.on('close', () => {\n   456→          maybeClose(this);\n   457→        });\n   458→      }\n   459→    }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  this.stdin = stdio.length >= 1 && stdio[0].socket !== undefined ?\n   463→    stdio[0].socket : null;\n   464→  this.stdout = stdio.length >= 2 && stdio[1].socket !== undefined ?\n   465→    stdio[1].socket : null;\n   466→  this.stderr = stdio.length >= 3 && stdio[2].socket !== undefined ?\n   467→    stdio[2].socket : null;\n   468→\n   469→  this.stdio = [];\n   470→\n   471→  for (i = 0; i < stdio.length; i++)\n   472→    ArrayPrototypePush(this.stdio,\n   473→                       stdio[i].socket === undefined ? null : stdio[i].socket);\n   474→\n   475→  // Add .send() method and start listening for IPC data\n   476→  if (ipc !== undefined) setupChannel(this, ipc, serialization);\n   477→\n   478→  return err;\n   479→};\n   480→\n   481→\n   482→function onErrorNT(self, err) {\n   483→  self._handle.onexit(err);\n   484→}\n   485→\n   486→\n   487→function onSpawnNT(self) {\n   488→  self.emit('spawn');\n   489→}\n   490→\n   491→\n   492→ChildProcess.prototype.kill = function(sig) {\n   493→\n   494→  const signal = sig === 0 ? sig :\n   495→    convertToValidSignal(sig === undefined ? 'SIGTERM' : sig);\n   496→\n   497→  if (this._handle) {\n   498→    const err = this._handle.kill(signal);\n   499→    if (err === 0) {\n   500→      /* Success. */\n   501→      this.killed = true;\n   502→      return true;\n   503→    }\n   504→    if (err === UV_ESRCH) {\n   505→      /* Already dead. */\n   506→    } else if (err === UV_EINVAL || err === UV_ENOSYS) {\n   507→      /* The underlying platform doesn't support this signal. */\n   508→      throw new ErrnoException(err, 'kill');\n   509→    } else {\n   510→      /* Other error, almost certainly EPERM. */\n   511→      this.emit('error', new ErrnoException(err, 'kill'));\n   512→    }\n   513→  }\n   514→\n   515→  /* Kill didn't succeed. */\n   516→  return false;\n   517→};\n   518→\n   519→ChildProcess.prototype[SymbolDispose] = function() {\n   520→  if (!this.killed) {\n   521→    this.kill();\n   522→  }\n   523→};\n   524→\n   525→\n   526→ChildProcess.prototype.ref = function() {\n   527→  if (this._handle) this._handle.ref();\n   528→};\n   529→\n   530→\n   531→ChildProcess.prototype.unref = function() {\n   532→  if (this._handle) this._handle.unref();\n   533→};\n   534→\n   535→class Control extends EventEmitter {\n   536→  #channel = null;\n   537→  #refs = 0;\n   538→  #refExplicitlySet = false;\n   539→\n   540→  constructor(channel) {\n   541→    super();\n   542→    this.#channel = channel;\n   543→    this[kPendingMessages] = [];\n   544→  }\n   545→\n   546→  // The methods keeping track of the counter are being used to track the\n   547→  // listener count on the child process object as well as when writes are\n   548→  // in progress. this.channel);\n\n    if (message === undefined)\n      throw new ERR_MISSING_ARGS('message');\n\n    // Non-serializable messages should not reach the remote\n    // end point; as any failure in the typeof message !== 'object' &&\n        typeof message !== 'number' &&\n        typeof message !== 'boolean') {\n      throw new ERR_INVALID_ARG_TYPE(\n        'message', ['string', 'object', null,\n        msg: message,\n      };\n\n      if (handle instanceof net.Socket) {\n        message.type = 'net.Socket';\n      } else if (handle instanceof net.Server) {\n        message.type = 'net.Server';\n      } else if (handle instanceof TCP || handle instanceof Pipe) {\n        message.type = 'net.Native';\n      } else if (handle instanceof dgram.Socket) {\n        message.type = 'dgram.Socket';\n      } else if (handle instanceof UDP) {\n        message.type = 'dgram.Native';\n      } else {\n        throw new ERR_INVALID_HANDLE_TYPE();\n      }\n\n      // Queue-up message options: options,\n          message: message.msg,\n        });\n        return this._handleQueue.length === 1;\n      }\n\n      obj = handleConversion[message.type];\n\n      // convert TCP object ArrayPrototypePush(this._handleQueue, {\n        callback: callback,\n        handle: null,\n        options: options,\n        message: message,\n      });\n      return this._handleQueue.length === 1;\n    }\n\n    const req = new WriteWrap();\n\n    const err = writeChannelMessage(channel, req, message, handle);\n    const wasAsyncWrite = streamBaseState[kLastWriteWasAsync];\n\n    if (err === 0) {\n      if (handle) {\n        this._handleQueue ||= [];\n        if (obj?.postSend)\n          obj.postSend(message, handle, options, callback, target);\n      }\n\n      if (wasAsyncWrite) {\n The three states are distinguished as follows:\n  // - disconnect() never requested: channel is not null and connected\n  //   is true\n  // - disconnect() requested, messages in the queue: channel is not null\n  //   and connected is false\n  // - disconnect() requested, channel actually disconnected: channel is\n  //   null and connected is false\n  target.connected = true;\n\n  target.disconnect = function() {\n    if (!this.connected) {\n      this.emit('error', new ERR_IPC_DISCONNECTED());\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Do not allow any new messages to be written.\n    this.connected = false;\n\n    // If there are no queued messages, disconnect immediately.
